The hotel rooms are spacious, well-equipped, clean and tidy, the shower has a large amount of water, and there is an independent small balcony. We had a comfortable foot bath massage in the afternoon after climbing the mountain, and a free dinner was also provided. It was really a surprise! I will definitely check in again in the future, and I hope the hotel will get better and better!
